It is almost certain that they are descended from the European family of Jass games, which originated in the Netherlands. Probably they were brought to the Indian subcontinent by Dutch traders.\r\n\r\n29 is a very addictive strategy card game.\r\n\r\nThe objective of the game is to be the first team to reach 6 points.\r\n\r\n29 card game is usually played by four players in fixed partnerships, partners facing each other. 32 cards from a standard 52-card pack are used for play. There are eight cards in each of the usual French suits: Hearts, Diamonds, Clubs and spades. In 29 card game the cards in every suit rank from high to low: J-9-A-10-K-Q-8-7.\r\n\r\nThe player need to bid and set a target for themselves and then achieve it. The player who wins the bid get to set the trump suit. Play is typically counter-clockwise; the player to the right of the dealer plays to the first trick. Players must follow suit if they have a card of the suit led, otherwise they must play a trump if possible.\r\nThe winner of each trick leads to the next. After the hand has been played, a score is taken based on the point values of the cards in the tricks each player has managed to capture. The aim of the game is to win tricks containing valuable cards.\r\n\r\nThe values of the cards are:\r\n\r\nJacks = 3 points each\r\nNines = 2 points each\r\nAces = 1 point each\r\nTens = 1 point each\r\nOther cards = (K, Q, 8, 7) no points\r\n\r\nRefine your skills and play against intelligent computer opponents in this fun 29 card game.\r\n\r\nNeed a fun card game for a family party or friendly get together?
